He was 48.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eBorn in Kiev, Ukraine in 1973, Zev\xe2\x80\x99s family immigrated the United States in 1977 and settled in Sheepshead Bay, Brooklyn, New York.\\u0026nbsp;\\u0026nbsp;\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eHe attended Hofstra University where he earned with a B.S. in chemistry with high honors.\\u0026nbsp; As a physician who masterfully combined the skills of both critical thinking and the scientific method, and who shaped their application out of his love for both God and patients, Zev was not content to sit back and wait for politicians or public health officials to settle upon a prescribed treatment path.\\u0026nbsp; People were dying.\\u0026nbsp; He began searching almost immediately for a method of treatment.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eAided by initiative, good fortune, and from his account divine intervention, he discovered such a treatment in combining Hydroxychloroquine (HCQ), zinc, azithromycin, and other various drugs, especially steroids, and creating what has come to be known as the \xe2\x80\x9cZelenko protocol.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u0026nbsp; The key to the protocol was very early intervention to treat the virus inside the cellular level before it could break loose and develop into a full-blown respiratory disease.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eUp to the time of his death, Zev had overseen the treatment of approximately 7,500 patients using his protocol and experienced only three patient deaths.\\u0026nbsp; The use of the Zelenko protocol has spread worldwide.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eWhile he was nominated along with other courageous doctors for a Nobel Prize in recognition of his groundbreaking treatment and outspoken advocacy on behalf of patients, for the most part Zev faced censorship and condemnation for his taking a bold stand against prevailing orthodoxy.\\u0026nbsp; This is a significant and historical victory in the medical freedom movement and directly affects federal employees subject to vaccine mandates.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eAFLDS is proud to have been part of this historical ruling. You can view the entire amicus curiae brief at the link below.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eWhat is a hearing en banc?\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eIt is very difficult to achieve a rehearing en banc. In fact, it is highly unusual and rarely ever granted. \\"En banc\\" is French for \xe2\x80\x9con the bench.\xe2\x80\x9d In the U.S. Circuit courts, a three-judge panel is generally assigned to hear arguments. A remedy for parties after a decision is rendered by a threejudge panel is to file a petition for a rehearing en banc. If a hearing en banc is granted, the entire Circuit Court will sit for a rehearing of the oral arguments and will determine whether the original ruling was correct.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eThe Federal Rules of Appellate Procedure, Rule 35 (A) states, in part:\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eAn en banc hearing or rehearing is not favored and ordinarily will not be ordered unless:\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003col style=\\"list-style-type:decimal;\\"\\u003e\\u003cli\\u003een banc consideration is necessary to secure or maintain uniformity of the court\'s decisions; or\\u003c/li\\u003e\\u003cli\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003ethe proceeding involves a question of exceptional importance1.\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/li\\u003e\\u003c/ol\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eIn the Feds for Medical Freedom case, a panel opinion was issued on April 7, 2022. That opinion, which declined jurisdiction over the federal employee vaccine mandate challenge, was vacated by\\u003cbr\\u003ethe Court\xe2\x80\x99s Order of June 27, 2022. The case will be reheard by the court en banc. Appellants will file an en banc brief on July 27, 2022. Appellees brief is due on August 26, 2022.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eThe case will be heard sometime during the week of September 12, 2022. He has shared his views over a broad spectrum of web-based podcast interviews and at numerous live appearances across the country.\\u0026nbsp; He has been routinely greeted with applause interruptions and standing ovations.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eAs to the rare form of cancer with which he was diagnosed in early 2018 and told of its 100 percent terminal prognosis, Zev repeatedly referred to it as having been a gift from God.\\u0026nbsp; \xe2\x80\x9cMy cancer is what prepared me for the Covid-19 pandemic,\xe2\x80\x9d He would say.\\u0026nbsp; \xe2\x80\x9cWithout it, I would not have developed my passion for searching for answers that others said couldn\xe2\x80\x99t be found, and without it I could not have held to the persecution and ridicule I received for daring to treat patients.\\u0026nbsp; I have looked death in the eye and I have been made ready to meet God.\\u0026nbsp; I fear nothing on this earth.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eA man of profound faith, he believed until the end that God had created a special mission for him on this earth, and that the prayers of millions had kept him alive long enough to fulfill that mission.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eZev recently announced the formation of his new Z Freedom Foundation, dedicated to continuing his critical work.\\u0026nbsp; He also announced the release of his memoirs, titled simply Zelenko, that will be available in late-summer to early fall 2022.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eHe is survived by his wife, Rinat, their two children, Shira and Liba, and six children from his previous marriage, Levi Yitzchok, Esther Tova, Eta Devorah, Nochum Dovid, Shmuel Nosson Yaakov, Menachem Mendel.\\u0026nbsp; Also his parents, Alex (Aaron) and Larisa (Leah) and his brother Ephraim (w. Chany).\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eIn his simple and beautiful poem, \\u003ci\\u003eHigh Flight\\u003c/i\\u003e, WWII Canadian Air Force pilot John Gillespie Magee said that he put out his hand, \xe2\x80\x9cand touched the face of God.\\u0026nbsp; For those who were blessed with having had a chance to cross paths, if even for a fleeting moment, with the remarkable man who was Vladimir \xe2\x80\x9cZev\xe2\x80\x9d Zelenko, there is a sense of knowing that in this instance and with all Guardsmen and Army Reservists to get vaccinated by COVID-19 or be dismissed. \\u0026nbsp;\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0px;\\"\\u003eAs pointed out by Rep. Mike Johnson (R-LA), the National Guard and Army Reserves\\u0026nbsp;are unlike other sectors in that their servicemen\\u0026nbsp;only serve part-time and typically have other sources of income. Therefore, the threat of dismissal may not hold the gravitas necessary to force members to get the injections.\\u0026nbsp;\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0px;\\"\\u003eAn estimated 13% of the National Guard remains unvaccinated, along with 10% of the Reserve. In some states, the unvaccinated make up 25% of the National Guard.\\u0026nbsp;\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0px;\\"\\u003eIf the National Guard loses a large chunk of its workforce, it may not be able to supplement those numbers. \xe2\x80\x9cZev\xe2\x80\x9d Zelenko\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:black!important;\\"\\u003eIt is with Dr. Zelenko was a physician, scientist, and activist for medical rights who touched the lives of millions of people. Some were saved as his role as a doctor, and even more were inspired by his words. His \\"Zelenko Protocol\\" saved millions and earned him a Nobel Prize nomination and the admiration of a U.S. President among other prominent world leaders.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:black!important;\\"\\u003eBorn in socialist slavery, and then immigrating to the United States, Dr. Zelenko was the embodiment of the American dream. The child of poor immigrants who rose to success as a physician and a businessman. But Dr. Zelenko was more than a physician. As an activist and a businessman, he was also a man of deep faith, incredible love for his family, and a tireless inspiration to the company. But, perhaps most of all, Zev was our friend. The world knows the dynamic firebrand who never feared speaking the truth to power or about issues he cared deeply about. Dr. Zelenko was a man of great, subtle humor and deep intellect.\\u0026nbsp; For every verbal jab he threw at the tired and incompetent establishment, a dozen more light-hearted laughs were spent with him and the team. Dr. Zelenko could laugh at himself as easily as others, and was always in great spirits, no matter the darkness that surrounded him - something that\'s easily overlooked in today\'s climate of hypersensitivity.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cdiv class=\\"raw-html-embed\\"\\u003e\\u003ciframe class=\\"rumble\\" width=\\"100%\\" height=\\"500\\" src=\\"https://rumble.com/embed/v15xjs9/?pub=4\\" frameborder=\\"0\\" allowfullscreen=\\"\\"\\u003e\\u003c/iframe\\u003e\\u003c/div\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:black!important;\\"\\u003eSome have already asked us what is next for Zelenko Labs. He was 48.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eBorn in Kiev, Ukraine in 1973, Zev\xe2\x80\x99s family immigrated the United States in 1977 and settled in Sheepshead Bay, Brooklyn, New York.\\u0026nbsp;\\u0026nbsp;\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eHe attended Hofstra University where he earned with a B.S. in chemistry with high honors.\\u0026nbsp; He then went on to the Buffalo School of Medicine where he earned his M.D. in 2000.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eZev had a family medical practice in Monroe, New York in 2020 during the onset of what would become the Covid-19 pandemic.\\u0026nbsp; As a physician who masterfully combined the skills of both critical thinking and the scientific method, and who shaped their application out of his love for both God and patients, Zev was not content to sit back and wait for politicians or public health officials to settle upon a prescribed treatment path.\\u0026nbsp; People were dying.\\u0026nbsp; He began searching almost immediately for a method of treatment.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eAided by initiative, good fortune, and from his account divine intervention, he discovered such a treatment in combining Hydroxychloroquine (HCQ), zinc, azithromycin, and other various drugs, especially steroids, and creating what has come to be known as the \xe2\x80\x9cZelenko protocol.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u0026nbsp; The key to the protocol was very early intervention to treat the virus inside the cellular level before it could break loose and develop into a full-blown respiratory disease.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eUp to the time of his death, Zev had overseen the treatment of approximately 7,500 patients using his protocol and experienced only three patient deaths.\\u0026nbsp; The use of the Zelenko protocol has spread worldwide.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eWhile he was nominated along with other courageous doctors for a Nobel Prize in recognition of his groundbreaking treatment and outspoken advocacy on behalf of patients, for the most part Zev faced censorship and condemnation for his taking a bold stand against prevailing orthodoxy.\\u0026nbsp; For whatever their motives, politicians and health officials worldwide attempted to either downplay or outright deny the efficacy of the Zelenko protocol and its simple, low-cost treatment path.\\u0026nbsp; Numerous studies were constructed to deliberately hide the effectives of using HCQ (later ivermectin) in conjunction with other drugs.\\u0026nbsp;\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eThere were even steps taken by politicians like then New York Governor Andrew Cuomo to forbid the use of HCQ in treating patients.\\u0026nbsp; Social media platforms joined in the effort to silence Zev, with Twitter having famously banned him from the platform in late 2020.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eAs Voltaire said, \xe2\x80\x9cIt is dangerous to be right in matters where established men are wrong.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eDespite numerous studies over the past two years that have supported the effectiveness of his protocol, access to the treatment remains denied to significant portions of the population and is simply ignored by many physicians.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eUndeterred, Zev went in search of another method to treat patients that could circumvent government restrictions.\\u0026nbsp; HE discovered that the natural supplement Quercetin could serve the same function as did HCQ in assisting zinc to attack the still developing virus inside the cell.\\u0026nbsp; It was not as effective, but as Zev was fond of saying, \xe2\x80\x9cYou don\xe2\x80\x99t go to war with the army you wish you had.\\u0026nbsp; You go to war with the army you\xe2\x80\x99ve got.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u0026nbsp; He discovery of Quercetin, which he likened to being a .22 caliber compared to HCQ\xe2\x80\x99s .50 caliber ultimately led to the development of his Z-Stack supplement.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cdiv class=\\"raw-html-embed\\"\\u003e\\u003ciframe class=\\"rumble\\" width=\\"100%\\" height=\\"500\\" src=\\"https://rumble.com/embed/vowxhh/?pub=4\\" frameborder=\\"0\\" allowfullscreen=\\"\\"\\u003e\\u003c/iframe\\u003e\\u003c/div\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eOver the past year-and-a-half, Zev has been an outspoken critic of the mRNA vaccine pointing to both its serious side-effects and its alteration of genetic code.\\u0026nbsp; He has been especially critical of the use of the vaccine in children who are not old enough to give their own informed consent and who face virtually no risk of serious illness from Covid-19.\\u0026nbsp; He has shared his views over a broad spectrum of web-based podcast interviews and at numerous live appearances across the country.\\u0026nbsp; He has been routinely greeted with applause interruptions and standing ovations.\\u003c/span\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp style=\\"margin-left:0in;\\"\\u003e\\u003cspan style=\\"color:inherit;\\"\\u003eAs to the rare form of cancer with which he was diagnosed in early 2018 and told of its 100 percent terminal prognosis, Zev repeatedly referred to it as having been a gift from God.\\u0026nbsp;
